	focus = {
		id = HOL_dutch_economic_landscape
		icon = dutch_windmill

		x = 10
		y = 0

		cost = 5

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ECONOMY }

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus HOL_dutch_economic_landscape"
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = HOL_dutch_economic_landscape
				category = CAT_3d
				category = CAT_genes
				category = CAT_computing_tech
				uses = 2
				bonus = 0.10
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					HOL_liberal_society_top_tier = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = gdp_per_capita }
				multiply_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.09 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = gdp_per_capita }
				multiply_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.10 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_active_mission = bankruptcy_incoming_collapse
			}
		}
	}
